3a1(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed
3a2(mdo sde): tshal mgon med zas sprin gyi kun dga' ra ba na/ dge slong gi dge 'dun

5a1(mdo sde): zla dang / rang na ba skyed rje nags pa dang / dang na

5a4(mdo sde): dang / tshe dang ldan pa legs 'ongs dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo
5a5(mdo sde): dang / de dag la sogs pa dge slong khri nyis stong dang thabs gcig
5b1(mdo sde): tu bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' sum khri nyis stong thams cad kyang skye ba gcig gis

6b3(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen po snying rje chen po sems pa dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sum khri nyis stong dang yang thabs
6b4(mdo sde): cig go// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod kyi grong khyer chen po na 'khor bzhi dang / rgyal po dang / rgyal po'i sras dang / rgyal
6b5(mdo sde): bo'i blon po chen po dang / chabs 'og gi rgyal phran dang / rgyal po'i zhabs 'bring ba dang / rgyal rigs dang / bram ze dang / tshong
6b6(mdo sde): dpon dang / khyim bdag dang / blon po dang / 'khor gyi mi dang / grong khyer dang / yul mi dang / mu stegs can dang / dge sbyong dang /
6b7(mdo sde): bram ze dang / spyod pa dang / kun tu rgya sna tshogs kyis rim gror byas/ bla mar byas/ bsti stang byas/ mchod pa byas so// bcom ldan
7a1(mdo sde): 'das ni bza' ba dang / bca' ba dang / myang ba gsod cing mang ba dang / na bza' dang / bsod snyoms dang / gzims cha dang /
7a2(mdo sde): sun gyi gsos sran dang / yo byad rung ba brnyes shing / bcom ldan 'das ni brnyes pa dam pa dang / grags pa dam pa brnyes kyang / pad ma la chus mi gos
7a3(mdo sde): pa ltar thams cad du yang ma chags ma gos par bzhugs so// bcom ldan 'das kyi grags pa dang / s+tha dang / snyan pa ni 'di skad du/
7a4(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das don de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs
7a5(mdo sde): ba/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo bsgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs
7a6(mdo sde): rgyas bcom ldan 'das zhes bya bar 'jig rten du mngon par grags par gyur to// de ni spyan snga dang ldan pa ste/ 'jig rten 'di dang /
7a7(mdo sde): 'jig rten pha rol lha dang bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang / bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu lha
7b1(mdo sde): dang mir bcas pa dag rang gi sa mngon par mkhyen pas mngon du mdzad nas nye bar bsgrubs te rab tu ston to// de thog mar dge ba bar du
7b2(mdo sde): dge ba/ tha mar dge ba/ don bzang po// tshig 'bru bzang po// ma 'dres pa/ yongs su rdzogs pa/ yongs su dag pa/ yongs su
7b3(mdo sde): dkar ba'i chos ston to// tshangs pa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston to// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis nam gyi gung 'thun la sangs rgyas kyis rgyan
7b4(mdo sde): bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin le snyoms par zhugs par gyur to// bcom ldan 'das kyis sangs rgyas kyi rgyan bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom
7b5(mdo sde): par zhugs ma thag tu/ skad cig de nyid la bcom ldan 'das kyis dbu'i gtsug gi gtsug tor gyi gseb nas/ sngon gyi sangs rgyas rjes su dran par bya ba la
7b6(mdo sde): chags pa med pa'i ye shes snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'od zer byung ste/ des gnas gtsang ma'i lha'i gnas thams cad snang bar byas nas/ lha'i bu dbang phyug
7b7(mdo sde): chen po la sogs pa lha'i bu tshad med pa yang dag par bskul to// de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od zer gyi tshogs de las bskul ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang
7b8(mdo sde): byung ngo // ye shes 'od ldan mun bcob 'od mdzad pa// 'od bzang gzi brjid dam pa dri med pa// sku lus rab zhi thugs dge zhi ba zo/
8a1(mdo sde): shAkya seng ge thub dang phrad par gyis// ye shes rgya mtsho thub chen dag pa ste// chos kyi mnga' bdag kun mkhyen
8a2(mdo sde): thub pa'i dbang // mi dang lha mchog lha yi lhar gyur pa// chos la rang byung mnga' dbang mdzad la rton// gang zhig sems la mnga' mdzad de// gang zhig
8a3(mdo sde): bdud kyi snyi las grol ba'i thugs// de 'dir mthong thos don med ma yin gyi// rnam grol mthar phyin zhi ba'i drung du deng // mtshungs med chos la snang bar gyur pa ste
8a4(mdo sde): mun sel tshul bzang ston par rab mdzad pa// sangs rgyas spyod ni mkhyen pa dpag med pa// de yi drung du dad pa mchog gis deng // de ni sman pa'i
8a5(mdo sde): rgyal po bdud rtsi gtong // de ni smra ba'i dpa' bo tshogs ngan 'joms// de ni chos rtsa lag don dam mkhas// de ni 'dren pa bla med lam ston pa'o//
8a6(mdo sde): gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag sngon gyi sangs rgyas rjes su dran par bya ba la chags pa med pa'i ye shes snang ba'i 'od zer des phog cing
8a7(mdo sde): tshigs su bcad pa rnam pa de dag gis kyang bskul ma thag tu rab tu zhi ba'i ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus bskal pa
8a8(mdo sde): grangs med/ tshad med/ bgrang ba las shin tu 'das pa dag las 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rjes su dran zhing sangs rgyas
8b1(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan bkod pa gang yin pa dag dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gang yin pa dag dang / chos bstan pa
8b2(mdo sde): gang yin pa de dag thams cad kyang rjes su dran par gyur to// de nas de'i nub mo mi nyal tsam na// gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu dbang phyug ces bya ba dang /
8b3(mdo sde): dbang phyug chen po dang / dga' bo dang / shin tu dga' bo dang / tsan dan dang / mchod byas dang / rab zhi dang / dul ba rab zhi dbang phyug la sogs pa de dag dang
8b4(mdo sde): gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu gzhan shin tu mang po kha dog 'phags shing / shin tu 'phags pa dang ldan pa dag gis lha'i snang bas rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal thams cad
8b5(mdo sde): snang bar byas te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der dong nas phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// phyogs
8b6(mdo sde): gcig tu 'khod nas kyang / gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rgya cher
8b7(mdo sde): rol pa zhes bgyi ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs mdo sde shin tu rgyas pa chen po smras pa/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yang

9a8(mdo sde): pad ma'i bla ma dang / chos kyi tog dang / mar me mdzad dang / yon tan gyi tog dang / yon tan 'byung gnas dang / 'od zer chen po dang /

12a6(mdo sde): tu gnas gyur la// rtse gcig sems su mnyam par bzhag drung du// rdzu 'phrul che zhing kha dog bzang ldan la// dri med dpal 'bar lha yi bu lhags nas/ dpal gyi

12a8(mdo sde): dang // shin tu dga' bo zhi ba lha yi bu// bya ba lha mang de dang de dag rnams// nga yi zhabs la phyag 'tshal bskor byas te// nga yi mdun du 'dir ni 'khod par/
12b1(mdo sde): 'gyur// sor mo de dag thal sbyar gus par bcas// de dag 'dir ni nga la gsol ba btab// 'jig rten kun la sbran pa'i don slad du// rgyal ba kun gyis sngon
12b2(mdo sde): chad gang gsungs pa// shin tu rgyas pa mdo gleng gzhi chen 'di// thub pas 'dod chags bstsal pas de ring yang // byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kun gzung
12b3(mdo sde): bzhed pas// phas kyi rgol dang bdud rnams 'dul mdzad la// theg pa chen po mchog 'dir rab gsung zhing // theg pa de slad legs par bshad du gsol/
12b4(mdo sde): lha yi tshogs kyis gsol ba de gnang phyir// mi gsung bas ni gnang ba mdzad pas na// thams cad tshim zhing rab dga' mgu gyur nas// dga' ba thob pas
12b5(mdo sde): me tog sil ma tor// de phyir dge slong dag kyang rgyas pa'i mdo// 'jig rten kun la phan pa'i don gyi phyir// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis sngon bshad pa// /

12b8(mdo sde): ldan gyi gnas mchog na gnas pa bye bas mchod pa// dbang bskur ba thob pa lha brgya stong gis bstod cing bkur te/ brjod cing bsngags pa bsam pa thob pa smon lam/
13a1(mdo sde): ces yang dag par 'phags pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par thob pa'i gro dang ldan pa/ ye shes kyi mig shin du yongs
13a2(mdo sde): su dag pa dang ldan pa// dran pa dang / blo gros dang / rtogs pa dang / khrel yod pa dang / dga' ba 'bar ba'i blo rlabs po che dang ldan pa/ sbyin pa dang / tshul
13a3(mdo sde): khrims dang / bzod pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang / shes rab dang / thabs la mkhas pa chen po'i pha rol du son pa/ tshangs pa'i lam byams
13a4(mdo sde): pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po dang / dga' ba dang / btang snyoms chen po la mkhas pa/ mngon par shes pa dang / rigs pa chen pos bsgrib pa med cing
13a5(mdo sde): chags pa med pa'i ye shes mthong ba mngon du gyur pa/ dran pa nye bar bzhag pa dang / yang dag par spong ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang / dbang po dang /
13a6(mdo sde): stobs dang / byang chub kyi yan lag dang / lam dang / byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad shin du yongs su rdzogs pa'i mthar phyin pa bsod nam
13a7(mdo sde): dang / ye shes kyi tshogs dpag tu med pa'i mtshan dang / dpe byad bzang pos lus legs par brgyan pa yun ring por rjes su 'brang ba dang ldan pa/
13a8(mdo sde): ji skad du smras pa de ltar byed pas logs med pa'i tshig gi las yang dag par smras pa/ drang zhing ma yol gya gyu med pa'i yid thogs pa med pa dang ldan pa/
13b1(mdo sde): nga rgyal dang / rgyags pa dang / dregs pa dang / 'jigs pa dang / zhum pa thams cad med pa/ sems can thams cad la sems mnyam pa/ sangs rgyas
13b2(mdo sde): bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong dpag tu med pa la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang pos ngor lta ba'i bzhin dang ldan pa/ brgya
13b3(mdo sde): byin dang / tshangs pa dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / 'jig rten skyong ba dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha'
13b4(mdo sde): lding dang / srin po rnams kyis mngon par dga' ba bya ba'i grags pa dang ldan pa/ tshig thams cad rab tu phye ste bstan pa la thogs pa med pa'i so so yang dag
13b5(mdo sde): par rig pa la 'jug pa'i shes pa la mkhas pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsungs pa/ gzung ba la dran pa'i snod 'khrugs pa med pa dang / gzung
13b6(mdo sde): mtha' yas mu med pa rab tu thob pa/ dran pa nye bar bzhag pa dang / yang dag par spong ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang / dbang po dang / stobs dang /
13b7(mdo sde): byang chub kyi yan lag dang / lam dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thabs mkhas pa'i chos rin po che dang / bsod nams kyis yang dag par
13b8(mdo sde): bsgrub pa'i chos kyi gru chen po'i ded dpon chen po chu bo bzhi'i pha rol du 'gro ba'i bsam pa can bdud dang phyir rgol ba bcom pa/ phas kyi rgol ba thams cad shin du tshar
14a1(mdo sde): bcad pa/ g.yul ngo'i thog ma la rab tu 'dug pa/ nyon mongs pa'i dgra'i tshogs 'joms pa/ ye shes mchog gi rdo rje'i/
14a2(mdo sde): mtshon sra ba dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi sems kyi rtsa ba las snying rje chen po'i chu bo lhag pa'i bsam pas skyes pa/ zab cing brtan pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi chos
14a3(mdo sde): kyi chus mngon par brlan pa/ thabs mkhas pa'i snying po dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bsam gtan gyi ze ba can/ ting nge 'dzin gyi ze 'bru dang
14a4(mdo sde): ldan pa/ yon tan gyi tshogs rgya chen po'i mtsho las skyes pa/ nga rgyal dang dregs pa'i gdung ba med pa'i zla ba med pa'i 'dab ma rgyas pa/ tshul khrims dang / thos
14a5(mdo sde): pa dang / bag yod pa'i gsung gi ngad phyogs bcur thogs pa med pa dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten na shes pas mthu bor gyur pa/ 'jig rten gyi chos brgyad kyis ma
14a6(mdo sde): gos pa/ skyes bu chen po pad ma bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi dri zhim po 'byung ba/ shes rab dang / ye shes kyi me'i 'od zer gyi mig shin tu rnam par dag pa'i
14a7(mdo sde): mdab me brgya pa rgyas pa/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bani mchog tu mgyogs pa'i shugs dang ldan pa/ 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'i sder mo dang / mche ba shin du rno ba/
14a8(mdo sde): tshangs pa'i gnas pa bzhi'i so drang bster ba/ bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhis shin du bsdus pa'i mgo dang ldan pa/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yan lag bcu gnyis po khong du/
14b1(mdo sde): chud pas/ rims kyis 'phags pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum bcu rtsa bdun yang dag par rdzogs pas ral pa can dus byas shing / rig
14b2(mdo sde): ba dang ye shes kyi ze ba can rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum gyi kha gdangs pa/ zhi gnas dang / lhag mthong shin du rnam par dag pa'i mig dang ldan pa/ bsam gta/
14b3(mdo sde): dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms pa'i 'jug pa'i ri sul gyi phug na gnas pa/ spyod lam bzhi dang / 'drul pa'i nags
14b4(mdo sde): tshal dang / nags 'dab nas skyes pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / nye ba'i stobs dang ldan pa/ skye ba
14b5(mdo sde): dang / 'jig pas 'jigs pa dang / spu g.yo ba med pas/ rtsal la zhum pa med pa/ mu stegs can gyi bung bu/ ri dwags mang po'i tshogs rab
14b6(mdo sde): tu 'joms pa/ bdag med par sgra brjod pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen po sgrogs pa/ skyes bu'i seng ge'i rnam par grol ba dang / bsam gtan gyi dkyil 'khor
14b7(mdo sde): las shes rab kyi 'od dang / 'od zer gyis mu stegs byed srin bu me khyer gyi tshogs 'od med par byed pa/ ma rig pa'i mun nag gi ling tog dang / rab
14b8(mdo sde): rib med par byed pa/ stobs dang / brtson 'grus 'bar ba/ lha dang mi'i nang du bsod nams kyi gzi brjid kyi gzi dang ldan pa/ skyes bu chen po'i
15a1(mdo sde): nyi ma nag zar phyogs med pa/ dkar po'i phyogs yongs su rdzogs pa/ lta na sdug cing yid du 'ong ba/ mig gi dbang na
15a2(mdo sde): la thogs pa med pa/ lha brgya stong gi skar ma'i tshogs kyis shin du brgyan pa/ bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor can dang /
15a3(mdo sde): byang chub kyi yan lag gi bde bas/ zla ba'i 'od zer du gyur pa/ mi dang lha mkhas pa'i me tog ku mu ta kha 'byed pa/ skyes bu chen po zla ba 'khor gyi gling bzhi
15a4(mdo sde): song ba/ byang chub kyi yan lag bdun gyi rin po che dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la sems mnyam par sbyor ba/ blo thogs pa med pa dge ba bcu'i las
15a5(mdo sde): kyi lam gyi dka' thub dang / brtul zhugs shin du phun sum tshogs shing rab tu rdzogs pas khyad par du bogs te byung ba rU ba'i bsam pa can/ chos kyi rgyal po'i
15a6(mdo sde): chos kyi 'khor lo rin po che'i mchog dam pa thogs pa med par bskor ba/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rigs kyi rgyud du byung ba/ chos kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba chen po
15a7(mdo sde): rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba/ zab cing gting dpag dka' ba/ chos rin po che thams cad kyis rab tu gang ba/ thos pas mi ngoms pas yangs shing
15a8(mdo sde): che la mtha' yas pa'i ye shes dang / tshul khrims kyi tshod las mi 'da' ba/ blo rgya mtsho dang sa ltar rgya che nga'i mchog tu gyur pa/ sa dang / rtswa dang / me dang /
15b1(mdo sde): rlung dang / mnyam pa'i sems su gyur pa/ ri rab ltar brtan zhing mi g.yo la/ bskyod par mi nus pa'i yid dang ldan pa/ rjes su chags pa dang / khong khro/
15b2(mdo sde): med pa nam mkha'i dkyil ltar dri ma med cing yangs la 'dra ba med par rgya che ba'i blo dang ldan pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pa shin du yongs su dag pa sbyin pa legs par byin pa
15b3(mdo sde): sngon sbyor ba legs par byas la/ lhags pa'i bya ba legs par byas pa/ bden pa'i rgyan gyis legs par brgyan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su
15b4(mdo sde): btsal bgos par bya ba bgos pa dge ba'i rtsa ba nges par byas pa/ bskal pa grangs med pa bdun du dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsgrubs pa/
15b5(mdo sde): sbyin pa rnam pa bdun byin pa bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po lnga la shin du sten pa legs par spyad pa/ lus kyis rnam gsum/ ngag gis rnam bzhi/ yid kyis
15b6(mdo sde): rnam gsum spyad par gyur pa/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bsten pa dang ldan pa/ yang dag pa'i sbyor ba yan lag bzhi bcu dang ldan pa sten par gyur pa/
15b7(mdo sde): yang dag pa'i smon lam yan lag bzhi bcu dang ldan pa smon lam btab pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pa yan lag bzhi bcu dang ldan pa la bzhugs pa/ yang dag pa'i
15b8(mdo sde): rnam par thar pa yan lag bzhi bcu dang ldan pa yongs su rdzogs par byas pa/ yang dag pa'i mos pa yan lag bzhi bcu dang ldan pa drang por byas pa/ sangs
16a1(mdo sde): rgya @rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag bzhi bcu'i rjes su rab tu byung ba/ sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong lnga bcu rtsa lnga la
16a2(mdo sde): sbyin pa bul ba/ rang sangs rgyas bye ba phrag phyed dang bzhi la lhag par bya ba byas pa/ sems can tshad med pa dag mtho ris dang thar pa'i lam du btsud par gyur pa/
16a3(mdo sde): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pa/ tshe gcig gos thogs pa 'di nas shi 'phos nas dga' ldan gyi gnas dam pa
16a4(mdo sde): na gnas pa/ lha'i bu dam pa tog dkar po zhes bya ba/ lha'i tshogs rnams kyis 'di ni 'di nas shi 'phos nas/ mi'i 'jig rten du skyes te/ ring po mi thog
16a5(mdo sde): par bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// zhes zer shin tu mchod pa gzhal med khang gnas sum khri nyis
16a6(mdo sde): stong rab tu gnas pa/ stegs bu dang / rta babs dang / skar khung dang / bsil khang dang / khang pa brtsegs pa dang / khyams kyis legs par
16a7(mdo sde): brgyan pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan bsgreng pa rin po che'i dril bu gser kha'i dra ba'i bla re bres pa/ me tog man da rab dang / man da rab
16a8(mdo sde): po chal par bkram pa/ lha'i bu mo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gru dbyangs len pa/ me tog a ti mug ta dang / tsam pa ka dang / skya snar dang / sa rtol dang /
16b1(mdo sde): btang bzung dang / btang bzung chen po dang / mya ngan tshang dang / n+ya gro ta dang / tin tu ka dang / a sa na dang / dong ka'i me tog dang / shing ke sa ra dang /
16b2(mdo sde): ta la dang / sa la dang rin pa'i shing ljon pa chen pos brgyan pa/ gser gyi dri bas g.yogs pa/ gzhi mnyam zhing bkod pas mdzes par byas pa/ me tog
16b3(mdo sde): snang 'od dang / ma li ka dang / sna ma'i me tog dang / bar shi ka dang / ta ra ni dang / ba li dang / go ta ra dang / mchog tu dri zhim dang / da nus ka ri
16b4(mdo sde): dang / lha'i sna ma'i me tog dang / ud pa la dang / pad ma dang / ku mu ta dang / pad ma dkar po dang / dri rab tu zhim pa'i bla re chen po phyogs phyogs su
16b5(mdo sde): bres pa/ bya 'dab spen dang / ne tse dang / ri skeg dang / khu byug dang / ngang pa dang / rma bya dang / dur pa dang / ku na la dang / ka la bing ka dang
16b6(mdo sde): shang shang de'u la sogs pa bya sna tshogs sgra snyan pa 'byin pa/ lha bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gis mig mngon du phyogs te/ lta zhing ltad mor bya ba chos rgya che ba chen
16b7(mdo sde): po yang dag par rdzogs pa 'dod pa la dga' ba'i shugs kyis nyon mongs pa thams cad gcod pa/ nga rgyal dang / dregs pa dang / khro ba dang / 'thab dang /
16b8(mdo sde): khong khro ba med par gyur pa dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / mchog tu dga' ba dang / dran pa rgya che zhing gsal ba skye ba'i gzhal med khang chen po de na/ bde
17a1(mdo sde): gnas shing / chos kyi yang dag pa'i gtam 'byung ba dang / sil snyan dang / glu dbyangs brgya khri bzhi stong pa'i sgra de dag las/
17a2(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa'i sngon gyi dge ba'i tshogs kyis yang dag par bskul ba'i tshogs su bcad pa 'di dag byung ngo // bsod nams rgya che tshogs mang dran rtogs dang //
17a3(mdo sde): blo gros mtha' yas shes rab 'od mdzad pa// mtshungs med stobs mnga' sku rtsal rgya che ba// mar me mdzad kyis lung bstan dgongs par mdzod//
17a4(mdo sde): rgya chen dri ma med pa'i thugs mnga' ba// dri ma gsum spangs rgyags dang skyon zhi ba// dge ba dri med rnam par dag pa'i thugs// sngon chad ji lta sbyin spyad
17a5(mdo sde): dgongs par mdzod// zhi gnas tshul khrims brtul zhugs bzod pa dang // dul dang brtson 'grus bsam gtan shes rab stobs// bskal pa bye ba khrag
17a6(mdo sde): khrig rnams spyad pa// spyod rig chen 'byung dgongs mdzod dgongs par mdzad do// sems can rnams la thugs brtser mdzad gyur cing // sangs
17a7(mdo sde): rgyas bye ba khrag khrig mchod kyis mchod// dgongs mdzod dgongs par mdzod cig grags mtha' yas// deng dus lags kyis btang snyoms ma mdzad cig/
17a8(mdo sde): rga shi nyon mongs 'jig mdzad rdul bral ba// lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dri za dang // lha min mang po dag ni sdod lags kyi// 'chi 'pho'i tshul mkhyen 'pho ba
17b1(mdo sde): bstan par mdzod// bskal pa stong du bka' ba spyang gyur kyang // rgya mtsho chu yis ji bzhin mi ngoms kyis// ngoms pa khyod kyis thugs dam dge ba ste/
17b2(mdo sde): yun ring skom nyen skye bo tshim par mdzod// smad pa med pa'i grags pa mnga' ba khyod// chos la dgyes pas khyod dgyes 'dod mi dgyes// 'on kyang dri ma
17b3(mdo sde): med pa'i spyan mnga' ba// lhar bcas 'jig rten dag la thugs brtse mdzad// lha rnams bye ba khyod las chos thos pas// ngoms par gyur pa ma lag
17b4(mdo sde): 'on gyis kyang // ngal dang mi ldan gyur pa'i ngan song du// gnas par gyur pa dag la gzigs su gsol// dri ma med pa'i spyan mnga' phyogs bcu yi//
17b5(mdo sde): 'jig rten dag gi sangs rgyas gzigs gyur cing // de dag rnams las chos gsan chos mchog de// 'jig rten dag la rnam par dbye ba mdzod//
17b6(mdo sde): dpal ldan khyod kyis bsod nams dpal gyis ni// dga' ldan pho brang shin tu mdzes mod kyi// 'on kyang thugs rje'i thugs dang ldan pas na// 'tsha
17b7(mdo sde): bu'i rgyal mtshan du ni char pa 'ob// brtul zhugs grub pa byang chub reg ces te// 'dod pa'i khams las rab tu 'das pa yis// gzugs kyi khams
17b8(mdo sde): na lha rnams gang khod pa// du ma thams cad mngon par rab tu dga'// mgon po khyod kyis bdud kyi las rnams bcom// khyod gzhan mu stegs can
18a1(mdo sde): rnams phab mdzad de// khyod ni byang chub phyag mthil bzhag dang 'dra// deng dus lags kyis btang snyoms ma mdzad cig/
18a2(mdo sde): nyon mongs me rab 'bar ba'i 'jig rten la// dpa' bo khyod kyis sprin ltar khyab mdzad de// bdud rtsi'i char pa mngon par rab tu phog/ lha mi rnams
18a3(mdo sde): kyi nyon mongs zhi bar mdzod// khyod ni sman pa mkhas la mkhas pa ste// yun rings nad pa sman pas bor ba yi// sems can rnam thar gsum gyi sbyar sman gyis//
18a4(mdo sde): mya ngan 'das pa'i bde la myur du 'khod// seng ge'i nga ro'i smra ba ma gyur pas// wa rnams 'jigs pa med par sgra sgrog gi/ sangs rgyas seng ge'i sgra ni rab
18a5(mdo sde): sgrogs te// mu stegs can gzhan wa rnams bsgrag par mdzod// sa yi dkyil na stobs dang brtson 'grus kyis// stobs ldan phyag na shes rab sgron ma bsnam/
18a6(mdo sde): phyag mthil dam pas sa la rngub mdzad de// 'di rnams khyod kyis rab tu pham par mdzod// gang dag khyod la lhung zed 'bul ba yi// 'jig rten skyong
18a7(mdo sde): ba bzhi po sdod cing mchis// khyod bskams yang dag len par 'gyur ba yi// brgya byin tshangs pakhrag khrig sdod cing mchis// tho gros bzang po rigs ca
18a8(mdo sde): rigs ldan pa// gang la gnas nas byang chub sems dpa' yi// spyod pa ston gyur dam pa rigs skyes pa// rigs kyi nang na btsun pa'i rigs la gzigs//
18b1(mdo sde): snod gyur gang du nor bu rin po che// gzhan na dpal dang ldan par 'gyur ba bzhin// nor bu rin chen lta bur dri med thugs// 'dzam bu'i rgyal mtshan du ni char pa pog/
18b2(mdo sde): glu dbyangs sgra las rnam pa 'di lta yi// tshigs su bcad pa mang po byung gyur na// 'di ni dus lags btang snyoms ma mdzad ces// snying rje'i yid dang ldan la bskul
18b3(mdo sde): bar byed// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dus de lta bus yang dag par bskul ba dang / gzhal med khang chen po de nas byung ste// chos kyi
18b4(mdo sde): mtho ba zhes bya ba'i khang bzangs der gang du byang chub sems dpa' 'dug cing dga' ldan gyi lha rnams la chos ston pa der// byang chub sems dpa' zhugs so//
18b5(mdo sde): zhugs nas kyang seng ge'i khri chos bzang po zhes bya ba la 'dug go/ de nas lha'i bu gang dag byang chub sems dpa' dang skal ba mnyam pa/ theg pa mtshungs pa la
18b6(mdo sde): zhugs pa de dag kyang khang bzang de nyid du zhugs so// gang yang byang chub sems dpa' phyogs bcu nas 'dus pa byang chub sems dpa' dang spyod pa 'dra ba dag
18b7(mdo sde): dang / lha'i bu de dag thams cad dang lha'i bu mo'i tshogs rnams stsal cing / lha'i bu pal rnams kyang stsal nas lhag pa'i bsam pa 'thun pa'i 'khor can du byas
18b8(mdo sde): te/ 'khor bye ba phrag drug bcu rtsa brgyad dang / khang bzangs der zhugs nas so so tsa rogs par rang rang gi seng ge'i khri la 'khod par gyur to// dge slong
19a1(mdo sde): dag de ltar lo bcu gnyis na byang chub sems dpa' ma'i mngal du 'jug par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tshe/ gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi
19a2(mdo sde): lha'i bu dag 'dzam bu'i gling du lhags nas lha'i kha dog mi snang bar byas te/ bram ze'i cha byad du bsgyur nas/ bram ze rnams rig byed slob du 'dzud de/ gang
19a3(mdo sde): zhig rnam pa 'di lta bur gyur na/ de ni skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan par 'gyur te/ de'i rin po che sna bdun ni 'di lta ste/ 'khor lo rin po
19a4(mdo sde): che dang / glang po rin po che dang / rta rin po che dang / bud med rin po che dang / nor bu rin po che dang / khyim bdag rin po che dang / blon po rI dang bdun no//
19a5(mdo sde): 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po'i 'khor lo rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan par 'gyur zhe na/ 'di la rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba/ gso sbyong gi nyi
19a6(mdo sde): mches bco lnga la mgo khrus byas te/ dbu zungs su gnas shing / steng gi khyams na bud med kyi tshogs kyis kun nas bskor cing 'dug pa'i tshe/ shar phyogs nas lha'i
19a7(mdo sde): 'khor lo rin po rtsibs stong yod pa/ mu mkhyud dang ldan pa/ lte ba dang bcas pa thams cad gser las grub pa/ mgar bas ma byas pa/ 'bang du shing ta la
19a8(mdo sde): bdun tsam na 'dug ste/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur bas/ lha'i 'khor lo rin po che de mthong nas 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis thos pa rgyal po

19b2(mdo sde): nas bskor nas 'dug pa'i tshe/ shar phyogs nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che 'byung bar 'gyur na/ de ni 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ro zhes thos na/
19b3(mdo sde): bdag gi drung du lha'i 'khor lo rin po che 'ongs pa las na/ bdag kyang 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po yin du nges so snyam ste/ de nas rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi
19b4(mdo sde): bo nas dbang bskur ba des/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ lag pa g.yas pas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che
19b5(mdo sde): de bskor cing 'di skad du/ btsun pa lha'i 'khor lo rin po che chos kyi 'khor lo bskor cig chos ma yin pas ni ma yin no zhes bya ba'i tshig sbas pa dang / de nas lha'i
19b6(mdo sde): 'khor lo rin po che de/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur bas rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkha' las shar phyogs su legs par 'gro ste/ rgyal po 'khor
19b7(mdo sde): los bsgyur ba yang dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu rjes su 'gro'o// sa'i phyogs gang du lha'i 'khor lo rin po che de gnas par gyur pa der/
19b8(mdo sde): rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba de yang / dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu gnas par 'gyur ro// de nas shar phyogs kyi
20a1(mdo sde): khams kyi rgyal po gang yin pa de dag dngul gyi snod ni gser byes bkang ste thogs/ gser gyi snod ni dngul sil mas bkang ste

20a3(mdo sde): srid ni shin tu 'byor la bde ste/ lo legs shing nyams dgyes la/ skye bo mang po dang mis bltam pa lags na/ lha nyid kyis yul du byon nas bzhugs su gsol
20a4(mdo sde): de skad ces spras pa dang / rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur bas/ khams kyi rgyal po de dag la 'di skad du/ khyed rang rang gi rgyal srid dag
20a5(mdo sde): chos bzhin gyis shig/ chos ma yin pas ni ma yin no// khyed srog chags ma gsod cig/ ma byin par ma len cig/ 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa ma byed
20a6(mdo sde): cig/ brdzun 'du ma smra shig/ phra mam zer shig/ dag rtsub po ma smra shig/ tshig rkyal ba ma smra shig/ brnab sems can du ma gyur cig/ gnod sems/
20a7(mdo sde): can du ma gyur cig/ log par lta bar ma gyur cig/ srog gcod pa la byams par ma gyur cig/ log par lta ba can gyi ba re la byams par ma byed cig/ nga'i yul
20a8(mdo sde): du chos ma yin pa byung nga re/ chos ma yin pa spyod pa la byams par ma byed cig ces bsgo nas/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur bas/ de ltar shar
20b1(mdo sde): phyogs su rnam par rgyal bar byed do// shar phyogs kyi rgyal bar byas nas/ shar phyogs kyi rgya mtsho la 'gro'o// shar phyogs kyi rgya mtsho la song nas/ shar phyog/
20b2(mdo sde): kyi rgya mtsho la rgal lo// rgal nas kyang lho phyogs su nam mkha' las rdzu 'phrul gyi legs par 'gro ste/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po yang dpung gi tshogs yan
20b3(mdo sde): lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu 'gro'o// snga ma bzhin du lho phyogs su rnam par rgyal bar byed do// lho phyogs su ji lta ba bzhini du/ nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs
20b4(mdo sde): su rnam par rgyal bar byed do// byang phyogs su rnam par rgyal bar byas nas/ byang phyogs kyi rgya mtsho la 'gro'o// byang phyogs kyi rgya mtsho la song nas/
20b5(mdo sde): byang phyogs kyi rgya mtsho las rgal lo// rgal nas kyang nam mkha' las rdzu 'phrul gyis rgyal po'i pho brang du legs par 'ongs nas/ btsun mo'i 'khor gyi
20b6(mdo sde): sgo'i steng du ma nyams par gnas te/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba ni/ 'khor lo rin po che rnam pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yin no// 'khor
20b7(mdo sde): los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po glang po rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i glang po rin po che snga ma bzhin du
20b8(mdo sde): 'byung ste/ thams cad thal dkar du gyur pa/ yan lag bdun shin du gnas pa/ gtsug gser gyis brgyan pa/ gser gyi rgyal mtshan dang ldan pa/
21a1(mdo sde): @#gser gyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser gyi dra bas g.yogs pa/ rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa/ nam mkha' las 'gro ba
21a2(mdo sde): rnam par 'phrul ba'i chos can te/ 'di ltar glang po'i byang chub ces bya'o// gang gi tshe rgyal po rgyal rigs skye bo nas dbang bskur ba/ glang po rin po che de
21a3(mdo sde): rtag par 'dod par gyur pa de'i tshe/ nyi ma shar kar glang po rin po che de la zhon te/ sa chen po 'di rgya mtsho'i mtha' skor dang / rgya mtsho'i mur thug pa dang bcas pa
21a4(mdo sde): kun du skor te/ rgyal po'i pho brang du 'ongs nas/ khye'u skus kyi dga' ba myong bar byed de/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ni/ glang po rin po che rnam
21a5(mdo sde): pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yin no// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rta rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas
21a6(mdo sde): dbang bskur ba'i rta rin po che snga ma bzhin du 'byung ste/ thams cad du sngon por gyur pa/ mgo gnag pa/ rnga ma lcang lor 'dug pa/ zhon na gus par
21a7(mdo sde): byed pa/ gser gyi rgyal mtshan dang bcas pa/ gser gyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ gser gyi dra bas g.yogs pa/ rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa/ na mkha' las
21a8(mdo sde): 'gro ba/ rnam par 'phrul pa'i chos can te/ 'di ltar rta'i rgyal po sprin gyi shugs can zhes bya'o// gang gi tshe rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba
21b1(mdo sde): rta rin po che rtag par 'dod par gyur pa de'i tshe/ nyi ma shar kar rta rin po che de la zhon nas/ sa chen po 'di rgya mtsho'i mtha' skor dang bcas pa/ rgya mtsho'i mur
21b2(mdo sde): thug pa dang bcas pa kun du bskor te/ phyir rgyal po'i pho brang du 'khor nas/ khye'u spus bde ba myong bar byed de/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ni
21b3(mdo sde): rta rin po che rnam pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yin no// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po nor bu rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la rgyal po rgyal
21b4(mdo sde): rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i nor bu rin po che snga ma bzhin du 'byung ste/ thams cad du bsngo ba bai DUr+ya'i rang bzhin can/ zur brgyad du 'dug pa/
21b5(mdo sde): shin tu sbyangs pa 'byung ste/ nor bu rin po che de'i 'od kyis btsun mo'i 'khor thams cad kyang snang bas khyab par gyur to// gang gi tshe rgyal po rgyal rigs
21b6(mdo sde): spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba nor bu rin po che de brtag par 'dod par gyur pa de'i tshe/ mtshan mo nam gyi gung la mun pa mun nag gi nang du/ nor bu rin po che de
21b7(mdo sde): rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo la btags te/ bskyed mos tshal gyi sa bzang po blta ba'i phyir song na/ nor bu rin po che'i 'od kyis thams cad dang ldan pa'i dpung gi
21b8(mdo sde): tshogs yan lag bzhi pa thams cad/ dpag tshad khor ra khor yug du snang bas gsal bar 'gyur ro// nor bu rin po che de'i 'khor na gnas pa'i mi de dag kyang
22a1(mdo sde): @#snang ba des gsal bar gyur pa dang / cig gis gcig mthong / gcig gis gcig shes nas/ cig la gcig 'di skad smra ste/
22a2(mdo sde): gzhin bzangs dag longs la las kyi mtha' dag byos shig/ tshong dus dag khrom/ nyi ma shar te nyin mor shes so zhes zer te/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas
22a3(mdo sde): dbang bskur ba de/ nor bu rin po che rnam pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yin no// rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba/ bud med rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang
22a4(mdo sde): ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i bud med rin po che snga ma bzhin du 'byung ste/ tshul dang 'thun pa/ rgyal rigs su skyes
22a5(mdo sde): pa/ ha cang yang mi ring ba/ ha cang yang mi thung ba/ ha cang yang mi sbom pa/ ha cang yang mi skem pa/ ha cang yang mi dkar ba/ ha cang yang mi gnag pa/
22a6(mdo sde): gzugs mdzes pa/ tshul du shis pa/ lta na sdug pa/ kha dog bzang po rgyas pa mchog dang ldan pa/ de'i spu'i khung bu thams cad nas tsan dan gyi dri 'byung ba/
22a7(mdo sde): kha nas ud pa la'i ngad ldan pa/ ka tsa lin da ltar reg na bde ba/ de grang ba'i dus na ni lus la reg na dro ba/ dro ba'i dus na lus la reg na bsil ba ste/
22a8(mdo sde): de 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ma gtogs pa/ gzhan la yid kyis kyang 'dod chags su mi byed na/ lus kyis lta ci smos te/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po
22b1(mdo sde): ni bud med rin po che rnam pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yin no// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po khyim bdag rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la rgyal po
22b2(mdo sde): rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i khyim bdag rin po che snga ma bzhin du 'byung ste/ mkhas pa/ gsal ba/ yid gzhungs pa/ lha'i mig dang ldan pa
22b3(mdo sde): 'byung ngo de lha'i mig des dpag tshad kho ra khor yug tu/ bdag po dang bcas pa'i gter dag kyang mthong / bdag po med pa'i gter dag kyang mthong ste/
22b4(mdo sde): de bdag po med pa'i gter gang yin pa de dag gis 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po'i nor gyi dgos pa byed de/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ni khyim bdag rin
22b5(mdo sde): po che rnam pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yin no// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po blon po rin po che rnam pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la 'khor los bsgyur
22b6(mdo sde): ba'i rgyal po'i blon po rin po che snga ma bzhin du 'byung ste/ mkhas shing gsal la yid gzhungs pa'o// de 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po des bsams
22b7(mdo sde): pa tsam gyis bskor bar dpung rnams bsgo'o// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ni blon po rin po che rnam pa de lta bu dang ldan pa yini te/ 'khor los bsgyur
22b8(mdo sde): ba'i rgyal po rin po che sna bdun de dag dang ldan pa yin no// de la bu stong 'byung ste/ dpa' ba/ brtul phod pa/ yan lag mchog gi gzugs dang ldan pa/
23a1(mdo sde): pha rol gyi sde rab tu 'joms pa sha stag ste/ des rgya mtsho la thugs pa'i sa chen po ma lus pa snod pa sngo ba med cing /
23a2(mdo sde): 'tshe ba med pa 'di nyid chad pa med cing mtshon gyis gda' ba med la/ chos kyis legs par phab ste gnas ste// gal te khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byung nas
23a3(mdo sde): sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/ 'dod pa'i 'dod chags sbyangs pa/ 'dren pa gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston par 'gyur ro zhes rig byed 'don
23a4(mdo sde): du 'dzud do// de bzhin du lha'i bu gzhan dag kyang 'dzam bu gling du lhags shing sangs rgyas dag la bskul ma 'debs te/ 'phags pa dag da ste lo bcu gnyis
23a5(mdo sde): na byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug gi/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di 'or cig ces zer ro// dge slong dag de'i tshe rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen
23a6(mdo sde): po na/ mjug ma bsgyur ba/ zhes bya ba'i ri la/ rang sangs rgyas glang po zhes bya ba 'dug pas sgra de thos nas/ rdo ba'i steng du 'jim pa la bya ba de bzhin du 'jug
23a7(mdo sde): ste/ nam mkha' la shing ta la bdun srid du 'phags so// gyen du 'phags nas kyang me'i khams la snyoms par zhugs te/ sgron ma bzhin du mya ngan las
23a8(mdo sde): 'das so// de'i mkhris pa dang bad kan dang / chu rgyus dang / rus pa dang / sha khrag tu gyur pa gang yin pa de thams cad ni mes yongs su zad par gyur te/
23b1(mdo sde): ring srel 'ba' zhig sa la lhags nas/ rkang rjes de dag ni da dung yang drang srong gis rjes su shes grag ste yod do// dge slong dag de'i tshe yul bA ra na se'i ri dgas
23b2(mdo sde): kyi nags drang srong lhung ba na// rang sangs rgyas lnga brgya 'khod pa de dag gis kyang sgra de thos nas/ nam mkha' la shing ta la bdun srid du gyen du 'phags nas
23b3(mdo sde): me'i khams la snyoms par zhugs te/ sgron ma bzhin du yongs su mya ngan las 'das so// de dag gi mkhris pa dang / bad kan dang / chu rgyus dang / rus pa
23b4(mdo sde): dang / sha dang khrag tu gyur pa gang yin pa de thams cad ni mi 'jigs pa byin pa'i ri dgas dag kyang de na gnas pas/ de phyin chad ri dgas kyi gnas shes bya ba yang /
23b5(mdo sde): ri dgas kyi gnas ri dgas kyi gnas shes ming du gyur to// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi gnas dam pa na 'dug pa ni/ lta ba chen po bzhi
23b6(mdo sde): la rnam par lta ste/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dus la rnam par lta ba dang / gling la rnam par lta ba dang / yul la rnam par lta ba dang / rigs la rnam par
23b7(mdo sde): lta ba'o// dge slong dag ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' dus la rnam par lta ba la rnam par lta ba zhes bye na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni thog ma'i dus sems can mi/
23b8(mdo sde): 'dul ba'i tshe ma'i mngal du mi 'jug gi/ gang gi tshe 'jig rten kun nas gsal bar gnas par 'gyur te/ skye ba snang bar gyur/ rga ba snang bar gyur/ na ba snang
24a1(mdo sde): bar gyur/ 'chi ba snang bar gyur pa de'i tshe/ byang chub sems dpa' ma'i mngal du 'jug go// dge slong dag ci'i phyir byang
24a2(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' gling rnam par blta ba rnam par lta zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni mtha' khob kyi gling du mi skye/ shar gyi lus 'phags por mi skye/ nub
24a3(mdo sde): ba lang spyod du mi skye/ byang sgra mi snyan du mi skye/ 'dzam bu gling nyid du skye'o// dge slong dag ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' yul rnam par lta ba la rnam
24a4(mdo sde): bar lta zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni mtha' khob kyi yul gang na/ mi rnams dbang po brtul zhing blun la lug ltar lkugs pa'i rang bzhin can/
24a5(mdo sde): legs par bstan pa dang nyes par bstan pa'i don shes par bya ba'i skal ba med pa dag yod pa dag tu mi skye'i/ byang chub sems dpa' ni yul gyi dbus nyid
24a6(mdo sde): du skye'o// dge slong dag ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rigs rnam par lta ba la rnam par lta zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni rigs dma' ba gdol pa'i
24a7(mdo sde): rigs sam/ sdig ma mkhan gyi rigs sam/ shing mkhan gyi rigs sam/ gaphung po'i rigs su mi spre'i/ bram ze'i rigs sam/ rgyal rigs kho na
24a8(mdo sde): ste/ de la gang gi tshe bram ze'i rigs btsun par bya ba de'i tshe/ bram ze'i rigs su skye'o// gang gi tshe rgyal rigs btsun par bya ba de'i tshe/ rgyal rigs su skye te/
24b1(mdo sde): dge slong dag da ltar ni btsun par byas na/ de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rgyal rigs su skye te/ dge slong dag don gyi dbang de la brten nas/ byang chub sems dpa'
24b2(mdo sde): dga' ldan gyi gnas dam pa na gnas pa/ rnam par lta ba chen po bzhi la rnam par lta ste/ de ltar ltas nas cang mi zer bar gyur to// dge slong dag de ltar lha'i
24b3(mdo sde): bu de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag cig la gcig 'di skad du/ byang chub sems dpa' rigs chen po ni ji lta ba bzhin du skye bar 'gyur/ yum ni ji
24b4(mdo sde): lta bu zhig gi lhums su 'jug par 'gyur zhes 'dri'o// de la la la na re yul ma ga ta ni lus 'phags kyi rigs 'di 'byor cing rgyas la lo legs pa dang / bde ba
24b5(mdo sde): dang ldan pa yin te/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la na re de ni tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin te/
24b6(mdo sde): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de ni ma'i rgyud kyis dag pa yang ma yin/ pha'i rgyud kyis dag pa yang ma yin la/ bsod nams chung ngus byung gi/ bsod
24b7(mdo sde): nams rgya chen pos mngon par byung ba ma yin zhing / rgod pa mi brtan te ma gnas pa yin la/ yul de yang nye 'khor gseg mas gang ba/ skyed mos
24b8(mdo sde): tshal dang / mtsho dang / mtshe'u dag kyang mi mang la/ ri brags ltar mtha' khob kyi gnas su gyur pa ste/ de'i phyir de ni tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin no zhes ze 'o//
25a1(mdo sde): @la la na re ko sa la'i rigs 'di 'khor mang zhing bzhon pa mngal nor che ba ste/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug
25a2(mdo sde): ba'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la na re de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar ko sa la'i rigs ni gdol ba'i rigs las
25a3(mdo sde): shi 'phos nas skyes pa yin te/ pha dang mas dag pa'ang ma yin la/ dma' ba la mos pa ste/ rigs mtho bar yang mi bya/ nor dang rin po che'i gter yang
25a4(mdo sde): tshad med par phun sum tshogs pa ma yin te/ de'i phyir de ni tshul dang mthun pa ma yin no zhes zer ro// la la na re bad sa la'i rigs 'di 'byor cing rgyas la lo leg
25a5(mdo sde): ba dang / bde ba dang ldan pa yin te/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la na re de yang tshul dang 'thun pa mi
25a6(mdo sde): yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar rgyal po bad sa la'i rigs ni phal pa ste/ gtum la gzi brjid 'bar ba yang ma yin zhing / skyes pa gzhan las skye ba
25a7(mdo sde): grub pa/ pha ma gnyis kyi gzi brjid kyi las kyis grub pa ma yin te/ de'i rgyal po yang chad par smra ba yin te/ de'i phyir de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin no zhes ze'o//
25a8(mdo sde): la la na re/ grong khyer chen po yangs pa can 'di ni/ 'byor cing rgyas la lo legs pa dang bde ba dang ldan pa yin te/ nyams dga' la skye bo mang po dang mis kun tu
25b1(mdo sde): gang ba/ stegs bu dang / bgam dang / rta babs dang / bsil khang dang / khang pa brtsegs pa dang / khang bzangs dag gis legs par brgyan pa ste
25b2(mdo sde): me tog gi ra ba dang / nags tshal gyi phreng ba me tog kun tu rgyas pa dang ldan pa yin la/ lha'i pho brang dang 'dra ba yin te/ de ni byang chub sems dpa'
25b3(mdo sde): yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la na re de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de dag la
25b4(mdo sde): ni phan tshun du rigs par smra ba med do// chos spyod pa med do// gong ma dang / bar ma dang / rgan pa dang / gtso bo dag la yang rim gro bya ba med cing /
25b5(mdo sde): re re zhing yang 'di snyam du bdag ni rgyal po'o// bdag ni rgyal po'o snyam du sems pas/ slob mar khas len pa med cing / chos khas len pa med ste/ de'i phyir
25b6(mdo sde): de yang tshul dang mthun pa ma yin no zhes zer ro// la la na re grong khyer 'phags rgyal na rab snang gi rigs 'di ni dpung che zhing bzhon pa mnga'/ pha rol gyi g.yul ngor
25b7(mdo sde): rgyal ba thob pa yin te/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la na re de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin te/
25b8(mdo sde): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de dag ni khro zhing gtum la rlang zhing bzung lum can rgod pa ste/ las yod par lta ba yang ma yin pas/ de'i phyir de yang byang chub sem
26a1(mdo sde): dpa' de lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas kyi 'os ma yin no zhes zer ro// la la na re grong khyer bcom brlag 'di 'byor zhing rgyas la/
26a2(mdo sde): lo legs pa dang / bde ba dang ldan pa/ skye bo mang po dang mis kun tu gang ba yin pas/ rgyal po lag bzangs ste dpa' ba'i bdag po'i rgyal po'i pho brang de ni/
26a3(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la na re de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/
26a4(mdo sde): 'di ltar rgyal po de ni log par lta ba'i rigs kyi rgyud du skyes pa ste/ mi rgod dang 'dra ba'i rgyal po yin pas/ byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma pa ni/
26a5(mdo sde): log par lta ba'i rigs su skye bar mi rigs te/ de'i phyir de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin no zhes zer ro// la la na re grong khyer ha sti na bur 'di'i rgyal po ni/
26a6(mdo sde): skya gser gyi bu'i rigs kyi rgyud las skyes pa/ dpa' zhing brtul phod pa dang ldan pa/ yan lag mchog gi gzugs phun sum tshogs pa/ gzhan gyi sde
26a7(mdo sde): 'joms pa ste/ rigs de ni byang chub sems dpa' de lhums su 'jug pa'i rigs kyi 'os yin no zhes zer ro// la la na re de yang tshul dang 'thun pa ma yin te/
26a8(mdo sde): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar skya gseng gi bu'i rigs su skyes pa dag gis ni/ rigs rgyud rnam par 'khrugs par byas te/ g.yul ngor brtan pa la ni chos kyi
26b1(mdo sde): bu zhes zer/ 'jigs sde la ni rlung gi bu zhes zer/ srid sgrub la ni dbang po'i bu zhes zer/ rigs med dang / lhar bcas la ni tha skar gyi bu zhe bya ste/
26b2(mdo sde): de'i phyir rigs de yang byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas kyi 'os ma yin no zhes zer ro// la la na re grong khyer bcom brlag 'di ni/
26b3(mdo sde): shin tu yang nyams dga' zhing phan tshun 'byed kyi/ rgyal po bzang po'i bshes gnyen bzhugs pa'i sa yang yin la/ rgyal po de yang glang po dang / rta dang /
26b4(mdo sde): shing rta dang / dpung bu chung dang / dpung gi tshogs mang po dang ldan pa/ gser dang / dngul dang / nor bu dang / mu tig dang / bai DUr+ya dang / dung dang /
26b5(mdo sde): man shel dang / sa le sbram dang / nor dang pho byad shin tu mang ba/ rgyal po dang / blon po thams cad kyi zil gyis mi non pa'i stobs dang pha rol gnon pa dang
26b6(mdo sde): ldan pa/ mdza' ba dang ldan zhing chos la dga' ste/ rigs de ni byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas su rung ngo zhes zer ro// la la
26b7(mdo sde): na re rgyal po bzang po'i gshes gnyen yon tan de lta bu dang ldan pa yod mod kyi/ de ni shin tu rgas pas bu skyed pa'i mthu yang med la/ bu yang mang bas
26b8(mdo sde): de'i phyir rigs de yang byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa'i gnas kyi 'os ma yin no zhes zer ro// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang /
27a1(mdo sde): lha de dag gis 'dzam bu'i gling gi yul chen po bcu drug po thams cad na/ rgyal po'i rigs mthon po gang ji snyed cig yod/
27a2(mdo sde): pa de dag thams cad la ltas na/ thams cad kyang nyes pa dang bcas par mthong ste/ de dag de ltar sems shin du la byed pa'i tshe/ lha'i bu ye shes tog gi
27a3(mdo sde): rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba/ byang chub las phyir mi ldog pa theg pa chen po 'di la nges par gyur pa zhig yod pa de/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor dang / lha'i 'khor
27a4(mdo sde): chen po yod pa de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// grogs po dag tshur sheg/ byang chub sems dpa' de nyid kyi drung du dong ste/ rigs rin po che yon tan ji
27a5(mdo sde): ltar phun sum tshogs pa zhig tu/ srid pa tha ma pa'i byang chub sems dpa' skye bar 'gyur ba dri'o zhes smras pa dang / legs so zhes te de dag thams cad kyang thal

27a8(mdo sde): ces smras so// grogs po dag byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma pa gang du skye bar 'gyur ba'i rigs de ni/ yon tan rnam pa drug bcu rtsa bzhi phun sum tshogs
27b1(mdo sde): pa yin te/ drug bcu rtsa bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rigs de ni btsun pa yin/ rigs de ni kun gyis mngon par shes pa yin/ rigs de ni phran tshegs
27b2(mdo sde): med cing gnod par byed pa med pa yin/ rigs de ni rgyud phun sum tshogs pa yin rigs de ni cho 'brang phun sum tshogs pa yin/ rigs de ni skyes bu zung phun
27b3(mdo sde): sum tshogs pa yin/ rigs de ni sngon gyi skyes bu zung phun sum tshogs pa yin/ rigs de ni btsun pa'i skyes bu zung phun sum tshogs pa yin/ rigs de ni
27b4(mdo sde): mngon par shes pa'i skyes du zung phun sum tshogs pa yin/ rigs de ni dbang che bar grags pa'i skyes bu zung phun sum tshogs pa yin/ rigs de ni skyes pa mang
27b5(mdo sde): ba yin/ rigs de ni bud med mang ba yin/ rigs de ni 'jigs pa med pa yin/ rigs de ni dman pa med cing zhum pa med pa yin/ rigs de ni

27b7(mdo sde): yin/ rigs de ni bzod don yod pas bshams shing longs spyod la spyod pa yin/ rigs de ni mdza' ba brtan pa yin/ rigs de ni dud 'gro'i skye gnas
27b8(mdo sde): su skyes pa'i srog chags kyi srog la lta ba yin/ rigs de ni byas pa bzo ba dang ldan pa yin/ rigs de ni brtul zhugs shes pa yin/ rigs de ni 'dun

28a3(mdo sde): yin/ rigs de ni bya ba la mos pa yin/ rigs de ni gtong ba la mos pa yin/ rigs de ni sbyin pa la mos pa yin/ rigs de ni zho sha shes pa yin//
28a4(mdo sde): rigs de ni rtsal brtan pa yin/ rigs de ni mthu rtsal dang ldan pa yin/ rigs de ni rtsa la mchog dang ldan pa yin/ rigs de ni drang srong mchod pa yin/
28a5(mdo sde): rigs de ni lha mchod pa yin/ rigs de ni mchod rten mchod pa yin/ rigs de ni mtshun rjed pa yin/ rigs de ni khon du 'dzin pa med pa yin/
28a6(mdo sde): yi de ni phyogs bcur grags pa yin/ rigs de ni 'khor chen po dang ldan pa yin/ rigs de ni 'khor mi byed pa dang ldan pa yin/ rigs de ni bla na med pa
28a7(mdo sde): 'khor dang ldan pa yin/ rigs de ni rigs kyi nang na gtso bor bya ba yin/ rigs de ni rigs la dbang thob pa yin/ rigs de ni rigs kyi dbang che bar
28a8(mdo sde): grags pa yin/ rigs de ni phar 'dzin pa yin/ rigs de ni mar 'dzin pa yin/ rigs de ni dge sbyong du 'dzin pa yin/ rigs de ni bram zer 'dzin pa yin//
28b1(mdo sde): rigs de ni nor dang 'bru'i dang mdzod mang ba yin/ rigs de ni dbyig dang / gser dang / nor dang / me tog dang / bai DUr+ya dang / dud dang / man shel
28b2(mdo sde): dang / sa le sbram dang / dngul dang / rdzas dang / yod byed mang ba yin/ rigs de ni glang po che dang / rta dang / rnga mo dang / ba lang dang / lug
28b3(mdo sde): shin tu mang ba yin/ rigs de ni bran po dang / bran mo dang / las byed pa dang / zho shas 'tsho ba shin tu mang ba yin/ rigs de ni thub par dka' ba yin/
28b4(mdo sde): rigs de ni don thams cad grub pa yin/ rigs de ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rigs kyi rgyud du skyes pa yin/ rigs de ni sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i grogs kyis
28b5(mdo sde): bskyed pa yin/ rigs de ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs su rigs btsun par skyes pa yin/ rigs de ni 'jig rten lha dang bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas
28b6(mdo sde): pa/ dge sbyong dang / bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu'i nang na/ rigs las smos pa'i skyon gyi kha na ma tho ba thams cad dang bral ba ste/ grogs po dag gang
28b7(mdo sde): du byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma pa 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i rigs de ni rnam pa drug bcu rtsa bzhi po de dag dang ldan pa yin no// grogs po dag srid pa tha ma pa'i
28b8(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' bud med gang zhig gi mngal du 'jug par 'gyur ba'i bud med de ni yon tan gyi rnam pa sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan pa yin te/ sum bcu rtsa
29a1(mdo sde): gnyis gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma pa ni/ kun gyis mngon par shes pa'i bud med kyi mngal/
29a2(mdo sde): du 'jug par 'gyur ro// kun gyis mngon par shes pa dang / spyod pa la glags mi thod pa dang / rigs phun sum tshogs pa dang / cho 'brang phun sum tshogs
29a3(mdo sde): pa dang / gzugs phun sum tshogs pa dang / ming phun sum tshogs pa dang / chu zheng phun sum tshogs pa dang / sngan chang bu ma btsas pa dang / tshul khrims phun
29a4(mdo sde): sum tshogs pa dang / gtong ba phun sum tshogs pa dang / gzhin 'dzum pa dang / 'thun par 'dzin pa dang / gang ba dang / dul ba dang / 'jigs pa med pa dang /

29a7(mdo sde): chung ba dang / bud med kyi sgron dang bral ba dang / khyim thab kyi brtul zhugs dang ldan pa dang / yon tan thams cad phun sum tshogs pa'i bud med kyi mngal du/
29a8(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tham pa 'jug go// grogs po dag byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma pa bud med gang gi mngal du 'jug pa'i bud med de ni yon tan gyi rnam
29b1(mdo sde): ba sum bcu rtsa gnyis po de dag dang ldan pa yin no// grogs po dag byang chub sems dpa' ni zla ba mar gyi ngo la ma'i mngal du mi 'jug gi byang chub sems dpa'
29b2(mdo sde): srid pa tha ma pa ni/ zla ba yar gyi tshes bco lnga'i zla ba nya ste rgyas pa la/ skar ma rgyal dang ldan pa'i tshe/ ma gso sbyong blangs pa'i mngal du 'jug go// de nas byang
29b3(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' de dag dang / lha'i bu de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' las/ rigs yongs su dag pa dang / ma yongs su dag pa'i rnam pa de lta bu de dag thos nas
29b4(mdo sde): 'di snyam du sems te/ skyes bu dam pa 'dis rnam pa ji snyam du bstan pa de lta bu'i yon tan dang ldan pa'i rigs de ni gang zhig yod snyam du sems so// de ltar sems shing
29b5(mdo sde): yid la byed pa la zhugs pa de dag 'di snyam ste/ shAkya'i grong 'di 'byor cing rgyas la bde zhing lo legs pa dang ldan te/ nyams dga' zhing skye bo dang mis gang ba yin la/
29b6(mdo sde): rgyal po zas gtsang ma yang ma'i rgyud kyis dag pa/ pho'i rgyud kyis dag pa dang / chung ma dag pa dang ldan pa dang / las kyi mtha' la nyon mongs pa med pa/ mnga' byed
29b7(mdo sde): bzang ba/ shin tu 'dzangs pa/ bsod nams kyi gzi brjid dang ldan pa/ grags pa chen po'i rigs su skyes pa/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rigs rgyud du skyes pa/
29b8(mdo sde): gter dang / rin po che dpag tu med pa dang ldan pa/ las yod par lta ba/ sdig pa'i lta ba med pa/ shAkya'i yul kun na yang rgyal po de gcig pur zad de/ tshong dpon dang /
30a1(mdo sde): khyib bdag dang / zon po dang / 'khor gyi mi thams cad kyis rim gro bya zhing mchod par mdzes pa/ lta na sdug pa/ ha cang yang mi rgan/
30a2(mdo sde): cang yang mi gzhon zhing gzugs mdzes la yon tan thams cad dang ldan pa/ bzo shes pa/ dus shes pa/ bdag shes pa/ chos shes pa/ sems can shes pa/

30a5(mdo sde): rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i bu mo zhig yod pa'ang / phyug cing gzhon zhing dar la bab pa'i gzugs phun sum tshogs pa/ sngan chad bu ma btsas pa/ bu dang bu mo med pa/
30a6(mdo sde): gzugs mdzes pa/ bu don la bris pa ltar lta na sdug pa/ lha'i bu mo ltar rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ bud med kyi skyon rnams dang bral ba/ bden par smra ba/
30a7(mdo sde): mi drag pa/ mi blang ba/ mi cor ba/ kha na ma tho ba med pa/ gyo mo'i sgra lta bu med pa/ caco med pa/ 'jam zhing sman la yid du 'ong bar smra ba/ mi nges pa dang / khong
30a8(mdo sde): khro ba dang / nga rgyal dang / dregs pa dang / rgyags pa dang / khro ba med pa/ brag dog med pa/ dus su sba ba/ gtong ba phun sum tshogs pa/ tshul khrims dang ldan pa/
30b1(mdo sde): khyos chog par 'dzin pa/ khyim thab kyi brtul zhugs can/ skyes pa gzhan las bsam pa'i yid la bya ba dang bral ba/ mgo dang / rna ba dang / sna gnas su phebs pa/

30b3(mdo sde): zhing snyan pa'i tshig dang ldan pa/ 'thun par 'dzin pa/ drang la gya gru med pa/ g.yo med pa/ khrel yod cing ngo tsha shes pa/ mi rgod pa/ mi g.yeng ba/ kha ngan mi smra
30b4(mdo sde): ba/ 'chal pa'i tshig med pa/ 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi shas chung ba/ dang des shing bzod pa dang ldan pa/ rkang lag dang / mig dang /

30b6(mdo sde): dbyibs legs shing mdog sdug pa/ yan lag shin tu brtag pa/ 'ja'i dbyibs ltar shin du 'dud pa/ yan lag dang nying lag shin tu 'byes pa/ yan lag la
30b7(mdo sde): slad du med pa/ mchu bim pa ltar dmar ba/ lta na mdzes pa/ mgul rim bzhin du 'dug pa/ rgyan dam pa dang ldan pa/ sna ma'i me tog dang / bar shi ka ltar so

31a1(mdo sde): nyams pa med pa/ lte ba khung zab pa/ sta zur 'jam zhing yangs pa/ zlum zhing brtan pa grub pa/ rdo rje ltar mkhregs

32b1(mdo sde): blta// sgyu 'phrul lha mo'i dge ba'i las kyi rgyus// rgyal po'i srid ni rab yangs rnam par 'phel// khams kyi rgyal po'ang 'jug par mi byed cing //

33a1(mdo sde): ris kyi lnga'i bu thams cad la sbas pa/ khyed rnams 'dir 'dug par gyis shig/ shi 'bo ba'i rnam par sbyor ba zhes bya ba

33a4(mdo sde): po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshad tsam du yangs par byin gyis brlabs par gyur nas/ de de tsam du bzang zhing de tsam du lta na sdug pa/ de tsam du rgyan gyi
33a5(mdo sde): rgyas shing de tsam du yid du 'ong bar gyur pa des/ 'dod pa na spyod pa dang / gzugs na spyod pa'i lha'i bu thams cad rang rang gi khyim gyi bkod pa la dur

33b1(mdo sde): dra bas g.yogs pa/ rin po che'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba du ma sgra byung bas mngon par dga' ba dang ldan pa/ rin po che'i dril bu brgya stong du ma mngon par dkrol/

33b3(mdo sde): du ma rab tu dpyangs pa/ dar gyi phreng ba lnga ldi brgya stong du mas shin du brgyan pa/ lha brgya stong du mas gru dbyangs gar byas rol mo byas pas yon tan brgya stong
33b4(mdo sde): du ma kun du brjod pa/ 'jig rten skyong ba brgya stong du mas rjes su bsrungs pa/ brgya byin brgya stong du mas phyag byas pa/ tshangs pa brgya stong du mas rab tu
33b5(mdo sde): btung pa/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag brgya stong du ma yongs su bzung ba/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma mtha' yas dgod
33b6(mdo sde): ba/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong dpag tu med par pha rol du phyin pa tshogs su byas pa'i bsod nams kyi rnam par smin pa'i rgyu 'thun pa las byung ba de lta
33b7(mdo sde): bu la 'dug go// dge slong dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i khri rten po yon tan de lta bu dang ldan pa la 'dug nas/ rtswa'i 'khor chen po de dag la

34a1(mdo sde): byang dang / 'og dang / steng dang / phyogs bcu kun na byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi gnas dam pa na 'khod cing //

34b1(mdo sde): par bya ba ste/ brgya rtsa brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ grogs po dag dad pa ni chos gnang ba'i sgo ste/ bsam pa mi phyed par 'gyur ro// dang ba ni chos
34b2(mdo sde): gnang ba'i sgo ste/ sems rnyog pa can dang bar 'gyur ro// mchog tu dga' ba ni chos gnang ba'i sgo ste/ las shin tu sbyangs par 'gyur ro// dga' ba ni
34b3(mdo sde): chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ sems rnam par dga' bar 'gyur ro// las kyi sdom pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ lus kyi nyes pa rnam pa gsum yongs su dag pa

35a3(mdo sde): btang snyoms ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ 'dod pa la smod par 'gyur ro// mi rtag par so sor rtog pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ 'dod pa dang / gzugs yod pa dang /

35a5(mdo sde): bdag med par so sor rtog pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ bdag tu mngon par zhen par med par 'gyur ro// zhi bar so sor rtog pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ rjes su chags

35a8(mdo sde): ba ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ chos la ston par 'gyur ro// gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ ngan song gsum las yang dag par 'da' bar 'gyuraro//
35b1(mdo sde): byas pa gzo ba ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba byas pa rnams chung mi za bar 'gyur ro// byas pa rig pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ gzhan la rnyas pa med par 'gyuraro//
35b2(mdo sde): bdag shes pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ bdag la bstod pa med par 'gyur ro// sems can shes pa ni chos snang ba sgo ste/ gzhan la smod pa med par 'gyur ro//
35b3(mdo sde): chos shes pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ chos kyi rjes su 'thun pa'i chos la nan tan byed par 'gyur ro// dus shes pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ mthong ba don yod par
35b4(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// nga rgyal bcom pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ ye shes yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// zhes 'gras pa med pa'i sems ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ bdag
35b5(mdo sde): dang gzhan rjes su bsrung bar 'gyur ro// 'khon du mi 'dzin pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ 'gyod pa med par 'gyur ro// mos pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ the tshom
35b6(mdo sde): med pa lhur len par 'gyur ro// mi sdug par so sor rtog pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ 'dod pa rnam par rtog pa spong bar 'gyur ro// gnod sems med pa ni chos snang
35b7(mdo sde): ba'i sgo ste/ gnod sems kyi rnam par rtog pa spong bar 'gyur ro// gti mug med pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ mi shes pa rnam par sel bar 'gyur ro// chos de
35b8(mdo sde): du gnyer ba ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ don la rton par 'gyur ro// chos 'dod pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ chos snang ba thob par 'gyur ro// thos pa tshol ba ni/
36a1(mdo sde): chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ tshul bzhin du chos la so sor rtog par 'gyur ro// yang dag pa'i sbyor ba ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste

36a4(mdo sde): snang ba'i sgo ste/ mtho bar sems pa med cing dpa' bar sems dpa' med par 'gyur ro// phung po la mkhas pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ sdug bsngal yongs

36a6(mdo sde): lam sgom par 'gyur ro// mi skye ba'i bzod pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ 'gog pa mngon du byed par 'gyur ro// lus la song ba'i dran pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/

36b1(mdo sde): dag par spong ba bzhi ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ mi dge ba'i chos thams cad spong ba dang / dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// rdzu 'phrul gyi rka/
36b2(mdo sde): ba bzhi ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ lus dang sems yang bar 'gyur ro// dad pa'i dbang po ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ shi na gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog par 'gyur ro//
36b3(mdo sde): brtson 'grus kyi dbang po ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ shin tu rtogs pa'i ye shes dang ldan par 'gyur ro// dran pa'i dbang po chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ las legs par/
36b4(mdo sde): byas par 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang po ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ sems rnam par grol bar 'gyur ro// shes rab kyi dbang po ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/
36b5(mdo sde): mngon sum gyi ye shes su 'gyur ro// dad pa'i stobs ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ bdud kyi stobs las yang dag par 'da' bar 'gyur ro// brtson 'grus kyi
36b6(mdo sde): stobs ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro// dran pa'i stobs ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ mi 'phrogs par 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin gyi

36b8(mdo sde): dran pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ chos ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes par 'gyur ro// chos rnam par 'byed pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan

38a1(mdo sde): 8@gyi sems can yongs su smin par byed par 'gyur ro// brtson 'grus pha rol tu phyin pa ni chos snang ba'i sgo ste/ dge ba'i chos

40b1(mdo sde): pas 'bad par gyis// la las byas shing sbyin pa yod ma yin// ma byas par yang 'grub par 'gyur ba med// sngon chad 'khor bar 'khor tshe sdug bsngal dag/

55a1(mdo sde): bdag gi rum du zhugs kyi de yis lo rgyus gsan par gsol// stong gsum khams 'di mdzes par rab rib ma mchis bdag
55a2(mdo sde): gis mthong // bdag ni nyal zhing mchis na lha rnams bye bas rab tu bstod// 'on kyang bdag la khro zhing 'tshig dang // zhe sdang rmongs ma mchis// zhi ba'i
55a3(mdo sde): sems su gyur cing bsam gtan bde dang ldan snyam bgyid// bdag gi rmi lam 'di ni rigs la dge 'am dngo 'am ci// bdag gi rmi lam yang dag ldan par lung
55a4(mdo sde): ston pa// rigs byed rmil pa gzhung la mkhas shing gzo yi cho ga mkhas// rgyal po myur du bram ze 'dir ni legs par dgug du gsol// de skad tshig thos
55a5(mdo sde): rgyal pos de yi dus kyi skad cig la// bram ze rigs byed bstan bcos gzhung la mkhas pa shin tu gnyer// sgyu 'phrul bram ze rnams kyi mdun du 'dug nas
55a6(mdo sde): 'di skad spras/ kho mos rmi lam 'di 'dra mthong na de yi lo rgyus gson// bram ze rnams kyis smras pa/ lha mo bka' stsal du gsol/ khyod kyi rmi lam 'di
55a7(mdo sde): 'dra ba cig gzigs/ thos nas kyang dpyad par bgyi'o// lha mos smras pa/ kha ba dngul gyi mdog 'dra nyi zla'i 'od las 'phags pa ste/ rkang lag legs
55a8(mdo sde): shing rab dbyes mche ba drug ldan che ba nyid/ glang po dam pa rdo rje bzhin du tshogs zhan gzugs bzang ba/ bdag gi rum du zhugs na de yi lo sbrus mnyan pa ba
55b1(mdo sde): de skad tshig thos nas ni bram ze rnams kyis 'di skad sras/ rigs la dbang ba ma mchis dges pa rgya chen brnyes par 'gyur// khyod la sras mnga' mtshan
55b2(mdo sde): gyis yan lag brgyan pa skye bar 'gyur// rgyal po'i rigs su rigs ldan 'khor los sgyur ba che ba nyid// gal te 'dod pa dag dang rgyal srid pho brang spangs
55b3(mdo sde): gyur te/ 'jig rten kun la thugs brtse chags med rab tu byung gyur na/ de ni 'jig rten gsum na sbyin gnas sangs rgyas 'byung ba ste/ bdud rtsi mchog
55b4(mdo sde): gi ro yis 'jig rten thams cad tshim mdzad 'gyur// de skad tshig snyan lung bstan te/ rgyal po'i pho brang zan zos nas/ bya dga' byin pa blangs nas su/
55b5(mdo sde): bram ze de dag phyir dong ngo // dge slong dag de ltar rgyal po zas gtsang mas bram ze mtshan dang ltas shes shing rnam par 'byed pa dang / rmi lam gzhung she
55b6(mdo sde): ba dag las 'di skad kyi tshig thos nas/ tshom zhing mgu ste yid rangs la/ rab tu dga' zhing dga' ba dang / yid bde ba skyes nas/ bram ze de dag
55b7(mdo sde): bza' ba dang / btung ba dang / myang ba mang po nyams su gsod pas tshim zhing ngoms par byas nas/ bya dga' byin te bkye'o// de nyid kyi tshe grong khyer
55b8(mdo sde): chen po ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po de'i sgo bzhin/ grong khyer gyi bzhi mdo dang / sum mdo thams cad du sbyin pa byin te/ ji tsam du byang chub sems
56a1(mdo sde): dpa' la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir/ zas 'dod pa rnams la zas/ skom 'dod pa rnams la ni skom/ gos 'dod pa rnams
56a2(mdo sde): la ni gos/ bzhon pa 'dod pa rnams la ni bzhon pa/ spos 'dod pa rnams la spos// phreng ba 'dod pa la rnams la ni phreng ba// byug pa 'dod pa rnams
56a3(mdo sde): la ni byug pa/ mal cha 'dod pa rnams la ni mal cha// gnas 'dod pa rnams la gnas/ 'tsho ba 'dod pa rnams la 'tsho ba sbyin no// dge slong dag de ltar
56a4(mdo sde): rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du sems te/ lha mo sgyu 'phrul 'di khyim gang na 'dug na bde zhing nyon mongs pa med par 'gyur snyam pa dang / de nas skad
56a5(mdo sde): cig de nyid la rgyal po chen po bzhi rgyal po zas gtsang mo'i drung du 'ongs te/ 'di skad ces smras so// lha thugs las su ma mdzad par btang snyoms
56a6(mdo sde): su bde bar bzhugs shig/ bdag cag gis byang chub sems dpa'i pho brang bsham mo// de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i
56a7(mdo sde): drung du 'ongs ste/ 'di skad ces smras so// skyong ba'i gzhal med khang rnams ngan/ sum bcu rtsa gsum pa yi bzang / byang chub sems dpa'i pho
56a8(mdo sde): brang ni/ rnam par rgyal tsam bdag gis dbul/ de nas lha'i bu rab 'thab bral byang chub sems dpa'i gan du 'ongs nas/ 'di skad ces smras so// /
56b1(mdo sde): kho bo'i khang khyim mthong gyur na// brgya byin bye ba ngo mtshar 'gyur/ 'thab bral rab kyi dpal ldan khang / rgyal ba'i sras la bdag 'bul lo//
56b2(mdo sde): de nas lha'i bu yongs su dga' ldan rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i gan du 'ongs te/ 'di skad ces smras so// grags pa che mnga' sngon chad ni/ dga' ldan gang du bzhug
56b3(mdo sde): gyur pa/ pho brang dam pa dges pa de// rgyal ba'i sras la bdag dbul lo// de nas lha'i bu rab 'phrul dga' rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i gan du 'ongs te 'di skad ces
56b4(mdo sde): sbas so// dpal ldan yid las grub pa'i khang // de ni rin chen rang bzhin te// byang chub sems dpa' mchog don du// rgyal po bdag gis dbul bar bgyi
56b5(mdo sde): de nas lha'i bu gzhan 'phrul dbang byed rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i gan du 'ongs te// 'di skad ces smras so// 'dod pa'i khams rnams ji snyed pa/ gzhal med
56b6(mdo sde): khang mdzes gang yod pa/ bdag gi gzhal med khang drung na// 'od dang mdog kyang ston par snang // des na dpal ldan bdag gis dbul// byang chub sems dpa'
56b7(mdo sde): mchod pa'i phyir// rin chen rang bzhin pho brang bzang // de ni rgyal po glang por gyis// lha yi me tog rab dkra ste// lha yi spos kyi ngad ldan pa'i// pho brang yangs
56b8(mdo sde): pa bdag gis dbul// der ni lha mo bzhugs par bgyis// dge slong dag de ltar 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha'i dbang po thams cad kyis// byang chub sems dpa' la mchod
57a1(mdo sde): pa bya ba'i phyir/ ser skya'i gnas kyi grong khyer chen po dam pa der rang rang gi khyim phul bar gyur to// rgyal po zas gtsang mas kyang /
57a2(mdo sde): mi'i las ni 'das kyi lha yir ma gyur pa gshams par gyur te/ de la byang chub sems dpa' bkod pa ting nge 'dzin gyi mthus/ khyim de dag thams cad du lha mo sgyu
57a3(mdo sde): 'phrul mngon par bstan to// byang chub sems dpa' lha mo sgyu 'phrul gyi rum na 'dug pa'i tshe/ glo g.yas phyogs logs su dkyil mo dkrung bcas te gnas par
57a4(mdo sde): gyur to// lha'i dbang po de dag thams cad kyang so so nas/ bdag nyid kyi khyim na byang chub sems dpa' 'dug gi/ gzhal de lta ma yin no zhes de ltar shes
57a5(mdo sde): par gyur to// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ ting 'dzin bkod pa che la gnas gyur te// sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab sprul byas nas// lha rnams thams cad
57a6(mdo sde): bsam pa rdzogs par byas// rgyal po 'ang de ltar yid bzhin bsams pa grub// de nas lha'i 'khor de'i nang nas lha'i bu kha cig 'di snyam du sems par gyur te/
57a7(mdo sde): rgyal chen bzhi'i rigs kyi lha gang yin pa de dag kyang / mi'i lus kyi dri bro na skyo zhing 'byol na/ de ma yin pa'i lha gzhan sum bcu rtsa gsum mam/ 'thab bral lam/
57a8(mdo sde): dga' ldan gyi lha'i bu dag lha mos kyang ci dgos na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' gtsang zhing dring ba dang bral ba/ 'jig rten thams cad las mngon par
57b1(mdo sde): 'phags pa/ sems can rin po che dga' ldan gyi lha'i ris nas 'phos te/ yum gyi lhums mi'i lus dri mi zhim par zhugs par gyur snyam pa dang / de nas sangs
57b2(mdo sde): rgyas kyi mthus// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji tsam du bud med lus ni smad pa lags pa
57b3(mdo sde): dang / 'dod chags la spyod ces bgyi ba'i bar du/ de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa ngo mtshar che na/ bcom ldan 'das de bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad
57b4(mdo sde): las mngon par 'phags pa/ sngon byang chub sems dpar gyur pa/ 'di ltar dga' ldan gyi lha'i ris nas 'phos te/ yum gyi lhums mi'i lus su glo g.yas
57b5(mdo sde): phyogs su bstan te bzhugs so// zhes bgyi ba 'di ni ngo mtshar te/ bcom ldan 'das/ sngon bcom ldan 'das kyis de ltar mdzad do// zhes/ de skad
57b6(mdo sde): smra bar ni bdag spro ba ma mchis so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo khyod byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa/
57b7(mdo sde): zhes bya ba/ gang byang chub sems dpa' ma'i ru pa na gnas pa'i yongs su spyad pa mthong bar 'dod dam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de'i dus ni de lag
57b8(mdo sde): bde bar gshegs pa de'i dus ni da lags te/ de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa de bstan te/ mthong na glo ba dga' 'o//
58a1(mdo sde): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rnam pa de lta bu'i mtshan ma mdzad de/ des mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pa/ tshangs pa 'bru
58a2(mdo sde): phrag drug bcu rtsa brgyad dang lhan cig tshangs pa'i 'jig rten nas mi snang bar gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis spyan sngar phyin nas/ des bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs
58a3(mdo sde): la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la bdud cing phyogs cig tu 'dug go//
58a4(mdo sde): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mkhyen bzhin du mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pa la bka' stsal pa/ tshangs pa khyod kyis sngon nga byang chub sems dpar gyur cing /
58a5(mdo sde): ma'i rum na zla ba bcur 'dug 'dug pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa blangs sam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de de ltar lags so//
58a6(mdo sde): bde bar gshegs pa de de lta lags so// dka' stsal pa/ tshangs pa da de ga la yod ston cig/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de ni tshangs pa'i 'jig rten
58a7(mdo sde): na mchis so// bka' stsal pa/ tshangs pa de'i phyir zla ba bcu pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa de 'dir khyod kyis ston cig dang / ji tsam du
58a8(mdo sde): 'dus byas pa shes par 'gyur ro// de nas mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pas/ tshangs pa dag la 'di skad ces sbas so// kho bos byang chub sems dpa'i
58b1(mdo sde): yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa de blang gi/ de'i bar du khyed 'khod cig/ de nas mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo/
58b2(mdo sde): bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan snga nas mi snang bar gyur nas/ skad cig de nyid la tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du phyin to// de nas mi mjed
58b3(mdo sde): kyi bdag po tshangs pas/ lha'i bu tshangs pa bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so// grogs po dag khyod song la tshangs pa'i 'jig rten man chad/ sum
58b4(mdo sde): sum rtsa gsum gyis gnas yan chad du sgra sgrogs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa/ bdag gis de bzhin gshegs
58b5(mdo sde): pa'i spyan sngar bkur na/ khyed kyi nang nas mthong bar su dga' ba myur du sheg shig ces sgras go bar bgyis shig/ de nas mi mjed kyi bdag po tshang
58b6(mdo sde): bas/ lha bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi dang lhan cig tu/ byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa blangs te/
58b7(mdo sde): tshangs pa'i gzhal med khang chen po dpag tshad sum brgya'i steng nas/ lha bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du mas kun nas bskor te/ 'dzam bu'i gling du phab po
58b8(mdo sde): de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi zham ring du 'dod pa na spod pa'i lha'i bu 'dus pa chen por gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa
59a1(mdo sde): #de yang / lha'i gos dang / lha'i phreng ba dang / lha'i spos dang / lha'i me tog dang / lha'i rol mo'i dbyang/

59a3(mdo sde): po brgya byin rgya mtsho'i dbus su 'dug nas/ rgyang ring po nas gdong thal mos skab te/ mgo bo nas ltas nas mthong bar ma nus so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/
59a4(mdo sde): lha'i nang na tshangs pa dag ni mthu che ste/ sum bcu rtsa gsum dang / 'thab bral dang / dge' ldan dang / 'phrul dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed
59a5(mdo sde): kyi lha dag kyang de dag gi drung na dma' ba yin na/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin lta mos kyang ci dgos/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe/ lha'i rol mo'i

59a7(mdo sde): po chen po bzhi lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyi drung du lhags nas/ 'di skad ces sbas so// lha'i dbang po byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa rin po che
59a8(mdo sde): bkod pa 'di bdag cag gis mthong bar mi nus na ji ltar bgyi/ des de dag la sbas pa/ grogs po dag kho bos ji ltar bya/ kho bo nyid kyis kyang je mtho
59b1(mdo sde): bar ma nus so// grogs po dag 'on kyang de ni bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar phul ba'i tshe mthong grang ngo // de dag gis sbas pa/ lha'i dbang po de bas na ci nas/
59b2(mdo sde): kyang myur du mthong bar 'gyur ba de ltar mdzad du gsol// smras pa grogs po dag lha'i mngon par 'phags pa de dag/ bdag bcom ldan 'das kyis spyan
59b3(mdo sde): sngar phyin te/ dga' bar bya ba'i tshig brjod kyi bar du sdod cig/ de nas phyogs cig tu 'khod nas/ mgo byo nas bcom ldan 'das logs su lta
59b4(mdo sde): zhing 'khod par gyur to// de nas mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pa/ lha bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi po de dag dang lhan cig tu/

59b6(mdo sde): yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa de ni/ gzugs bzang ba/ mdzes pa/ lta na sdug pa/ gru bzhi lham pa/ ka pa bzhi zug pa/ steng khang pa
59b7(mdo sde): brtsegs pas rgyan pa ste/ de'i tshad ni 'phang du 'di lta ste dper na/ byis pa btsas nas zla ba drug lon pa tsam mo// khang pa brtsegs pa de'i nang du
59b8(mdo sde): khri bshams pa ni 'di lta ste dper na/ byis pa btsas nas zla ba drug lon pa 'dug pa'i stegs bu tsam mo// byang chub sems dpa'i yongasu spyad par bya ba
60a1(mdo sde): rin po che bkod pa de'i kha dog dang dbyibs ni 'di lta bu ste/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten na de'i dbyibs dang kha
60a2(mdo sde): dog 'dra ba gang yang med do// lha rnams kyis de mthong na yang mi 'khrugs shing ngo mtshar du 'gyur ro// de de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan sngar

60a6(mdo sde): chen pos gos bgos pa de yang de'i drung na mdzes par mi snang ste/ 'di lta ste dper na/ rlung dang char gyis btab pa'i lAs ba nag po bzhin no//
60a7(mdo sde): khang pa brtsegs pa de ni can dan sbrul gyi snying po las byas pa ste/ de'i phye ma zho gcig la yang stong gi 'jig rten gyis rin du mi chog go// khang
60a8(mdo sde): ba brtsegs pa de ni tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po de lta bus kun nas/ bskor ba ste/ khang pa brtsegs pa de dang 'dra ba gnyis pa cig kyang / khab pa brtsegs
60b1(mdo sde): ba dang po de'i nang nam chags ma reg par 'dug go// khang pa brtsegs pa de kho na dang 'dra ba gsum pa cig kyang / khang pa brtsegs pa gnyis pa de'i nang
60b2(mdo sde): ma reg ma chags par 'dug go// spos kyi khang pa brtsegs pa de'i nang du khri de bzhag ste gdan bting ngo // tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po de'i kha dog ni rnam pa 'di
60b3(mdo sde): lta bu ste dper na/ bai DUr+ya sngon po rigs dam pa dang ldan pa bzhin no// spos kyi khang pa brtsegs pa de'i 'khor na/ me tog lha'i las 'das pa gang

60b5(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su spyad pa rin po che bkod pa de ni rdo rje'i rang bzhin te/ sra zhing brtan la mi shigs pa ste/ ka tsa lin da'i gos ltar reg na

60b7(mdo sde): rin po che bkod pa der kun tu snang ngo // gang gi nub mo byang chub sems dpa' ma'i rum du 'jug pa de'i nub mo 'og gi cha'i phung po nas bzung ste/ sa chen
60b8(mdo sde): po'i rngams dpag tshad 'bum phrag drug bcu rtsa brgyad brtol te/ pad ma byung nas/ tshangs pa'i 'jig rten gyi bar du mngon par 'phags so// pad+ma de ni/
61a1(mdo sde): kha lo sbyar ba skyes bu dam pa dang / tshangs pa chen po brgya phrag bcu'i stong la dbang bas mthong du zad kyi/ gzhan
61a2(mdo sde): sus kyang mthong ba med do// stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na nyid khu dang / snying po dang / bcud ji snyed yod pa de dag tham
61a3(mdo sde): cad pad ma chen po de la zil dngar gyi thigs par chags te 'dug nas/ de tshangs pa chen pos bai DUr+ya'i snod bzang pos blangs shig/ byang chub sems
61a4(mdo sde): dpa' la phul nas/ byang chub sems dpas kyang de blangs te/ tshangs pa chen po la snying brtse ba'i phyir 'thungs par gyur ro// snying khu'i thigs pa de

61b1(mdo sde): par me tog gi phud dang / 'bras bu'i phung dang / rol mo'i phud de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten rnams dang /
61b2(mdo sde): de bzhin gshegs pa'i nyan thos kyi dge 'dun rnams dang / pa dang ma la phul zhing phyis bdag nyid yongs su spyod pas/ las de'i rnam par smin pas/

111a5(mdo sde): D+ha zhes brjod pa dang yul la mi gtsang ba'i sgra byung ngo // Na zhes brjod pa dang nyon mongs pa ni phra ba'o zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // ta zhes brjod pa dang de bzhin
111a6(mdo sde): nyid ni ma 'dres pa'o zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // tha zhes brjod pa dang mthu stobs shugs dang / mi 'jigs pa'i sgra byung ngo // da zhes brjod pa dang sbyin
111a7(mdo sde): pa dang / dul ba dang / yang dag par sdom pa dang nges pa'i sgra byung ngo // d+ha zhes brjod pa dang 'phags pa rnams kyi nor ni rnam pa bdun no zhes bya ba'i sgra byung/
111a8(mdo sde): na zhes brjod pa dang ming dang gzugs yongs su shes par bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // pa zhes brjod pa dang don dam sgra byung ngo // pa zhes brjod pa dang 'bras bu rnyed
111b1(mdo sde): ba mngon du bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // ba zhes brjod pa dang bcings pa las rnam par thar pa'i sgra byung ngo // b+ha zhes brjod pa dang srid pa 'jig pa'i sgra byung ngo //
111b2(mdo sde): ma zhes brjod pa dang nga rgyal dang rgyags pa zhi bar bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // ya zhes brjod pa dang chos ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs par bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // ra zhes
111b3(mdo sde): brjod pa dang dga' ba med pa ni don dam par dga' ba zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // la zhes brjod pa dang 'khri shing chad pa'i sgra byung ngo // wa zhes brjod pa
111b4(mdo sde): dang theg pa mchog gi sgra byung ngo // sha zhes brjod pa dang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gi sgra byung ngo // Sha zhes brjod pa dang skye mched drug gzhon zhing mngon
111b5(mdo sde): par shes pa drug dang ye shes thob pa'i sgra byung ngo // sa shes brjod pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba'i sgra
111b6(mdo sde): byung ngo // ha zhes brjod pa dang nyon mongs pa bcom zhing 'dod chags dang bral ba'i sgra byung ngo // k+Sha zhes brjod pa dang yi ge mthar byin te chos thams ca
111b7(mdo sde): ni brjod du med pa'o zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ngo // de ltar byis pa de dag yi ge'i phyi mo slob pa'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i bathus de dag la sogs pa chos kyi sgo mo brkyang /
